         <script type="text/javascript">
          amzn.sx.utils.jsDepMgr.when('jQuery', 'deptRefinementCollapseExpand', function($) {
        
        function init(){
            setupView();
            addListeners();
        }

        function setupView(){
            $('#seeAllDepartmentClosed1').show();
            $('#fewDep').show();
            $('#seeAllDepartmentOpen1').hide();
        }

        function addListeners(){
            $showHideLinks.click( handleToggleLinkClick );
            $smartAPSSortUpdate.click( handleSmartAPSSortUpdate);
        }

        function handleToggleLinkClick( e ){
            var $el = $( e.currentTarget ),
                elToShow = $el.attr( "data-el-to-show"),
                elToHide = $el.attr( "data-el-to-hide");
            toggleElements( $( elToShow ),  $( elToHide ) );
            e.preventDefault();
            return false;
        }

        function handleSmartAPSSortUpdate(e){
            var dynamicID = $(e.currentTarget).attr("data-dynamic-id");
            smartAPSSortUpdate( dynamicID );
            e.preventDefault();
            return false;
        }

        function toggleElements( $toShow, $toHide ){
            $toHide.hide();
            $toShow.show();
        }

        
        var $showHideLinks = $(".s-hack-show-hide-el"),
            $smartAPSSortUpdate = $(".s-hack-smart-aps-sort-update");

        
        init();

    });
         </script>

    <script>
     'use strict';

!function() {
    if (!(window.P &amp;&amp; window.localStorage &amp;&amp; window.history)) {
        return;
    }
    
    var P90X = 'p90x',
        SEARCH_PATHS = ['/s', '/mn/search']; 
    function deleteP90XCookie() {
        var i;
        for (i = 0; i &lt; SEARCH_PATHS.length; i++) {
            window.document.cookie = P90X + '=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; path=' + SEARCH_PATHS[i] + ';';
        }
    }
    


    var PLUS_MATCHER = /\+/g,  
        PARAM_MATCHER = /([^&amp;=]+)=?([^&amp;]*)/g, 
        ONE_MINUTE = 1 * 60 * 1000, 
        ONE_DAY = 1 * 24 * 60 * ONE_MINUTE, 
        FIVE_DAYS = 5 * ONE_DAY, 
        UNCLASSIFIED = 'U', 
        FAST = 'F', 
        SLOW = 'S', 
        reqQ = [], 
        pbM = {}, 
        ielIdx = 0; 
    function nowMillis() {
        return + new Date();
    }
    
    
    function addNewLatencyRecRemoveOldRecs(p90x, isAjax, isNotPageOne, m) {
        var n = nowMillis(), l = p90x.l, h;
        
        
        if (!isAjax) {
            h = 'i';
        } else {
            if (isNotPageOne) {
                h = 'p';
            } else {
                h = 'm';
            }
        }
        
        
        l.unshift({'h': h, 'm': m, 't': n});
        
        
        while (l.length &amp;&amp;
                ((n - l[l.length - 1].t) &gt; FIVE_DAYS)) {
            l.pop();
        }
    }
    
    
    function makeClassificationRec(c, s) {
        return {'c': c, 's': s, 't': nowMillis()};
    }
    
    
    function getP90XFromLocalStorage() {
        var p90x = window.localStorage[P90X];
        if (p90x) {
            return JSON.parse(p90x);
        }
        
        
        return {'v': 'A', 'c': makeClassificationRec(UNCLASSIFIED, 0), 'l': []};
    }
    
    
    function setP90XIntoLocalStorage(p90x) {
        window.localStorage[P90X] = JSON.stringify(p90x);
    }
    
    
    function decode(s) {
        return decodeURIComponent(s.replace(PLUS_MATCHER, " "));
    }
    
    
    function getUrlParams(url) {
        var match, urlParams = {};
        while (match = PARAM_MATCHER.exec(url)) {
            urlParams[decode(match[1])] = decode(match[2]);
        }
        return urlParams;
    }

    
    function setP90XCookie(c, d) {
        var date = new Date(), i;
        date.setTime(nowMillis() + d);
        for (i = 0; i &lt; SEARCH_PATHS.length; i++) {
            
            window.document.cookie = P90X + '=A' + c.c + '; expires=' + date.toUTCString() + '; path=' + SEARCH_PATHS[i] + ';';
        }
    }
    
    
    function logP90XClassification(c) {
        var s = c.s;
        s = (s.toFixed(5) * 100000).toString().match(/[-]?(\d*)/)[1]; 
        ue.count('p90x-classification-score', s);
        ue.count('p90x-classification-score-negative', c.s &lt; 0 ? 1 : 0);
        ue.count('p90x-classification', c.c === SLOW ? 1 : 0);
    }
    
    
    function maintainP90XClassification(p90x, nC) {
        var d;
        
        p90x.c = nC;

        if (nC.c === SLOW) {
            
            d = ONE_MINUTE;
            while (d &lt; ONE_DAY &amp;&amp; classifyP90X(p90x, d * 2).c === SLOW) {
                d *= 2;
            }
            if (d &gt; ONE_DAY) {
                d = ONE_DAY;
            }
            
            setP90XCookie(nC, d);
        } else {
            deleteP90XCookie();
        }
        
        
        logP90XClassification(nC);
    }
    
    
    function classifyP90X(p90x, tO) {
        var i, l = p90x.l, s, h, n = nowMillis(),t, m;
        
        
        s = 0.0;
        for (i = 0; i &lt; l.length; i++) {
            h = l[i];
            t = n - h.t + tO; 
            m = h.m;
if (h.h === "p") {
    if ((t &gt;= 0) &amp;&amp; (t &lt; 60000) &amp;&amp; (m &gt;= 0.0) &amp;&amp; (m &lt; 100.0)) s += -0.550645;
    else if ((t &gt;= 0) &amp;&amp; (t &lt; 60000) &amp;&amp; (m &gt;= 10000.0) &amp;&amp; (m &lt; 11000.0)) s += 1.097729;
    else if ((t &gt;= 0) &amp;&amp; (t &lt; 60000) &amp;&amp; (m &gt;= 1000.0) &amp;&amp; (m &lt; 1200.0)) s += -0.194029;

    function updateP90X(isAjax, isNotPageOne, m) {
        var p90x = getP90XFromLocalStorage(), nC;
        
        addNewLatencyRecRemoveOldRecs(p90x, isAjax, isNotPageOne, m);
        nC = classifyP90X(p90x, 0);
        maintainP90XClassification(p90x, nC);
        
        setP90XIntoLocalStorage(p90x);
    }
    
    
    function doP90X() {
        var ue = window.ue, i, pb, pbParams, r, rem, m, isAjax, isNotPageOne;
        
        try {
            
            while (ielIdx &lt; ue.iel.length) {
                
                pb = decodeURIComponent(ue.iel[ielIdx++].src); 
                if (!pb.match(/http(s)?:\/\/fls-[^\$]*\$uedata=s:\/mn\/search\/uedata/i)) {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                pbParams = getUrlParams(pb);
                if (!(pbParams.hasOwnProperty('id') &amp;&amp; pbParams.hasOwnProperty('tc') &amp;&amp; pbParams.hasOwnProperty('cf'))) {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                pbM[pbParams.id] = pbParams;
            }
            
            
            rem = 0; 
            for (i = 0; i &lt; reqQ.length; i++) {
                r = reqQ[i];
                
                
                if (r === null) {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                pbParams = pbM[r.id];
                if (!pbParams) {
                     
                    rem = 1;
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                reqQ[i] = null;
                
                
                if (pbParams.bft) {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                if (isNaN(pbParams.tc) || isNaN(pbParams.cf)) {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                m = -1 * parseInt(pbParams.tc) + parseInt(pbParams.cf);
                if (m &lt; 0) {
                    continue; 
                }
    
                
                isAjax = pbParams.sc ? pbParams.sc.match(/^searchAjax/) !== null : false;
                isNotPageOne = r.url.match(/[\?&amp;]page=\d+/) !== null;
                
                
                updateP90X(isAjax, isNotPageOne, m);
            }
            
            
            if (rem) {
                
                setTimeout(doP90X, 500);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            window.ueLogError &amp;&amp; window.ueLogError(e, {'logLevel': 'ERROR', 'attribution': 'sx-p90x-fast-cookies'});
        }
    }
    
    
    function reqHandler() {
        var ue = window.ue;
        if (!ue || !ue.ctb || !ue.iel || !ue.id || !ue.count) {
            return;
        }

        
        reqQ.push({'id': ue.id, 'url': location.href});
        
        
        setTimeout(doP90X, 100);
    }
    
    
    window.P &amp;&amp; window.P.when('jQuery').execute(function ($) {
        $(window).load(reqHandler);
        $(document).bind("searchajax", reqHandler);
    });


    
}();
